4.1.1 Curated Educational Collection Page

A quick mock up of education's curated collection.

Example

Practical Solutions for LDL-C Reduction:An Education Curriculum
These educational resources are crafted to help clinicians enrolled in the TRANSFORM LDL-C Risk Initiative to understand nonstatin therapy options and equip clinical teams to overcome barriers to deliver them to patients.

Educational Path to Transforming LDL-C

  • Follow the Science: Refining Risk Assessment in ASCVD
  • Transforming LDL-C Risk: Role of Non-statin Therapies
  • Practical Tips for Prior Authorizations: A Discussion with the Experts
  • Coming Soon: Online Course: PCSK9 Inhibitors: The Who, What and Wow!
  • Coming Soon: MOD Capture of Clinical Curriculum from Washington, DC Event (title TBD)
  • Coming Soon: MOD of QI Champion Curriculum from Washington, DC Event (title TBD)
  • Coming Soon: An Interactive Infographic on Patient Risk Assessment and Identification for Intensification of LDL-C Therapies

2018 Guideline on the Management of Blood Cholesterol: Practical Applications

  • Follow the Science: Refining Risk Assessment in ASCVD
  • Transforming LDL-C Risk: Role of Non-statin Therapies
  • Practical Tips for Prior Authorizations: A Discussion with the Experts
  • Coming Soon: Online Course: PCSK9 Inhibitors: The Who, What and Wow!
  • Coming Soon: MOD Capture of Clinical Curriculum from Washington, DC Event (title TBD)
  • Coming Soon: MOD of QI Champion Curriculum from Washington, DC Event (title TBD)
  • Coming Soon: An Interactive Infographic on Patient Risk Assessment and Identification for Intensification of LDL-C Therapies
We are grateful to these distinguished Members of the American College of Cardiology who contributed to this collection.
  • Pamela B. Morris, MD, FACC, FAHA, FASPC, FNLA (Chair) Director, Seinsheimer Cardiovascular Health Program Co-Director, Women's Heart Care Medical University of South Carolina
  • Kim K. Birtcher, PharmD, MS, AACC, FNLA Clinical Professor University of Houston College of Pharmacy
  • Roger S. Blumenthal, MD, FACC Director, Ciccarone div for the Prevention of Cardiovascular Disease Johns Hopkins Hospital
  • Carl E. Orringer, MD, FACC Associate Professor of Medicine Director, Preventive Cardiovascular Medicine Cardiovascular Division University of Miami Miller School of Medicine
This initiative is a part of multi-project series developed by the ACC using data analytics, ACC clinical algorithms, and the PINNACLE Registry to focus and TRANSFORM the delivery of care for patients.

TRANSFORM LDL-C Risk is funded by Sanofi and Regeneron in partnership with the American College of Cardiology.
